Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 163, the first (unflown) release of the Apollo 14 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with reconstructed source code for Luminary 173. Changes between revision 163 and 173 were backed out, as described by Luminary memos 157 and 158. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152N. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those for the baseline log section mentioned in each file's changelog; the page numbers for a real Luminary 163 listing would be different.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

016910,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016911,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016912,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 163.
016913,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the first
016914,000006:                                                                                                  ##              (unflown) release of the flight software for the Lunar
016915,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 14.
016916,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a reconstructed copy of
016917,000009:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 173, as well as Luminary memos 157 amd 158.
016918,000010:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
016919,000011:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 163 in NASA
016920,000012:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021152N, which gives relatively high confidence
016921,000013:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
016922,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 395-479
016923,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016924,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016925,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
016926,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-21 MAS  Created from Luminary 173.

016929,000021:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016930,000022:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016931,000023:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016932,000024:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016933,000025: 
016934,000026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016935,000027: 
016936,000028:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016937,000029:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016938,000030:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016939,000031:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016940,000032:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016941,000033:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016942,000034:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016943,000035:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016944,000036:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016945,000037: 
016946,000038:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016947,000039:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
016948,000040:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016949,000041:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016950,000042:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016951,000043:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016952,000044: 
016953,000045: 
016954,000046:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
016955,000047: 
016956,000048:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016957,000049:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016958,000050:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016959,000051:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016960,000052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016961,000053: 
016962,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016963,000055:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016964,000056:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016965,000057:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016966,000058: 
016967,000059:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016968,000060:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016969,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016970,000062:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016971,000063:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016972,000064: 
016973,000065: 
016974,000066:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
016975,000067: 
016976,000068:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016977,000069:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016978,000070:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 396 

016980,000072:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016981,000073:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016982,000074:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016983,000075:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016984,000076:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016985,000077:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016986,000078:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016987,000079:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016988,000080:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016989,000081:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016990,000082: 
016991,000083:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016992,000084:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016993,000085:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016994,000086: 
016995,000087: 
016996,000088:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
016997,000089: 
016998,000090:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016999,000091:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017000,000092:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017001,000093: 
017002,000094:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017003,000095:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017004,000096:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017005,000097:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017006,000098:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017007,000099:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017008,000100:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017009,000101: 
017010,000102:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017011,000103:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017012,000104: 
017013,000105: 
017014,000106:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017015,000107: 
017016,000108:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017017,000109:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017018,000110:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017019,000111:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017020,000112: 
017021,000113: 
017022,000114:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017023,000115: 
017024,000116:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017025,000117:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017026,000118:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017027,000119:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017028,000120: 
017029,000121:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 397 

017031,000123:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017032,000124: 
017033,000125: 
017034,000126:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017035,000127: 
017036,000128:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017037,000129:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017038,000130: 
017039,000131:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017040,000132:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017041,000133:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017042,000134:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017043,000135: 
017044,000136:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017045,000137:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017046,000138: 
017047,000139:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017048,000140:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017049,000141:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017050,000142:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017051,000143: 
017052,000144:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017053,000145:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017054,000146: 
017055,000147:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017056,000148:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017057,000149: 
017058,000150:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017059,000151: 
017060,000152:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017061,000153:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017062,000154:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017063,000155:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017064,000156: 
017065,000157:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017066,000158:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017067,000159: 
017068,000160:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017069,000161:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017070,000162: 
017071,000163: 
017072,000164:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017073,000165:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017074,000166:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://www.ibiblio.org/apollo/hrst/archive/1706.pdf --- MAS 11/2016.)

017089,000181:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
017090,000182: 
017091,000183: 
017092,000184:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017093,000185: 
017094,000186:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017095,000187:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017096,000188:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017097,000189:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017098,000190:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017099,000191:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017100,000192:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017101,000193:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017102,000194:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017103,000195:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017104,000196:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017105,000197:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017106,000198:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017107,000199:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017108,000200:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017109,000201:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017110,000202:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017111,000203:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017112,000204:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017113,000205:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017114,000206:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017115,000207:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017116,000208:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
017117,000209:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017118,000210:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017119,000211:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017120,000212:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017121,000213:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017122,000214:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017123,000215:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017124,000216:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017125,000217:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017126,000218:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017127,000219:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017128,000220:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017129,000221:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017130,000222: 
017131,000223: 
017132,000224:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

017134,000226:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
017135,000227:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
017136,000228:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
017137,000229: 
017138,000230:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
017139,000231:                                                                                                  #  WDRET    =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
017140,000232:                                                                                                  #  DECRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
017141,000233:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG =      INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
017142,000234:

017144,000236:                                                                                                  #  CHAR     =      POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
017145,000237:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT    =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
017146,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT  =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
017147,000239: 
017148,000240:                                                                                                  #  SGNON    =      VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
017149,000241:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM  =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
017150,000242:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
017151,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
017152,000244: 
017153,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
017154,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017155,000247:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017156,000248:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017157,000249:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
017158,000250:                                                                                                  #  CODE     =      VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
017159,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
017160,000252:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN  =      VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017161,000253:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.
017162,000254:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP  =      VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
017163,000255:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017164,000256: 
017165,000257:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
017166,000258: 
017167,000259:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET   =      DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
017168,000260:

017171,000263:

017207,000299:

017209,000301:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017210,000302: 
017211,000303:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
017212,000304:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
017213,000305:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2

017216,000308:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION

(003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017248,000340: 
017249,000341: 
017250,000342:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017251,000343:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017252,000344:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017253,000345:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017254,000346:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017255,000347:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017256,000348: 
017257,000349:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017258,000350:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017259,000351:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017260,000352:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017261,000353:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017262,000354:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017263,000355: 
017264,000356:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017265,000357:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1    11       ALL ARE OCTAL
017266,000358:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2    10
017267,000359:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3    7
017268,000360:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4    6
017269,000361:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5    5
017270,000362:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1    4
017271,000363:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2    3
017272,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3    2
017273,000365:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4    1
017274,000366:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5    0
017275,000367:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017276,000368: 
017277,000369: 
017278,000370:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017279,000371: 
017280,000372:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017281,000373:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017282,000374:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017283,000375:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017284,000376:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017285,000377:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 402 

017287,000379:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017288,000380:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017289,000381:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017290,000382:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017291,000383:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017292,000384:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017293,000385:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017294,000386:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017295,000387:

Page 419 

018037,001129:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018038,001130:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018039,001131:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018040,001132:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018041,001133:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018042,001134:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018043,001135: 
018044,001136:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018045,001137:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018046,001138: 
018047,001139:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018048,001140: 
018049,001141:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018050,001142:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018051,001143:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018052,001144: 
018053,001145:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018054,001146:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018055,001147:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018056,001148:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018057,001149:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018058,001150:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018059,001151: 
018060,001152:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018061,001153:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018062,001154:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018063,001155:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018064,001156:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018065,001157: 
018066,001158:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018067,001159:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018068,001160:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018069,001161:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018070,001162:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018071,001163:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018072,001164:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018073,001165:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018074,001166: 
018075,001167: 
018076,001168:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018077,001169:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018078,001170:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018079,001171: 
018080,001172: 
018081,001173:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018082,001174:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018083,001175: 
018084,001176:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018085,001177:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018086,001178:

Page 420 

018088,001180:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS

018090,001182: 41,2363           02433                           TC       COMPTEST

019295,002387: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
019296,002388:

Page 445 

019298,002390:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019299,002391:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019300,002392:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019301,002393:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019302,002394:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019303,002395: 
019304,002396:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019305,002397:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019306,002398:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019307,002399:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019308,002400:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019309,002401:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019310,002402:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019311,002403: 
019312,002404:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019313,002405:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019314,002406:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019315,002407: 
019316,002408:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019317,002409:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019318,002410: 
019319,002411:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019320,002412:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019321,002413:

019450,002542:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019451,002543:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019452,002544:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
019453,002545: 
019454,002546:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019455,002547: 
019456,002548:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019457,002549:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019458,002550:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019459,002551: 
019460,002552:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019461,002553:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
019462,002554:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
019463,002555: 
019464,002556: 41,3405           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019465,002557: 41,3406           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019466,002558: 41,3407           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019467,002559: 41,3410           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
019468,002560: 41,3411           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
019469,002561: 41,3412           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
019470,002562: 41,3413           03415                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
019471,002563: 41,3414           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019892,002984:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
019893,002985:

Page 458 

019895,002987:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019896,002988: 
019897,002989:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019898,002990: 
019899,002991:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019900,002992:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019901,002993:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019902,002994:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019903,002995: 
019904,002996:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019905,002997:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019906,002998:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019907,002999: 
019908,003000:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019909,003001:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019910,003002:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019911,003003:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019912,003004:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019913,003005:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019914,003006:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
019915,003007:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019916,003008:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019917,003009:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019918,003010:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019919,003011: 
019920,003012: 40,3533           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019921,003013: 40,3534           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019922,003014: 40,3535           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019923,003015: 40,3536           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019924,003016: 40,3537           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019925,003017: 40,3540           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019926,003018: 40,3541           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019927,003019: 40,3542           03551                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019928,003020: 40,3543           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019929,003021: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019930,003022: 40,3545           03547                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019931,003023: 40,3546           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019932,003024: 40,3547           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019933,003025: 40,3550           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019934,003026: 40,3551           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019935,003027: 40,3552           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019936,003028: 40,3553           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019937,003029: 40,3554           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019938,003030: 40,3555           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019939,003031: 40,3556           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019940,003032: 
019941,003033: 40,3557                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019942,003034:

Page 459 

019944,003036:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019945,003037:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019946,003038:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019947,003039:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019948,003040:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019949,003041: 
019950,003042:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019951,003043:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019952,003044:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019953,003045: 
019954,003046:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019955,003047:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019956,003048: 
019957,003049:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019958,003050:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019959,003051:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019960,003052:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
019961,003053:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019962,003054: 
019963,003055:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019964,003056:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019965,003057:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019966,003058:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019967,003059: 
019968,003060:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019969,003061:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019970,003062:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019971,003063:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019972,003064:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019973,003065:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019974,003066:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019975,003067: 
019976,003068:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019977,003069:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019978,003070: 
019979,003071:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019980,003072:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019981,003073: 
019982,003074:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019983,003075:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019984,003076: 
019985,003077:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019986,003078:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019987,003079:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019988,003080:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019989,003081:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019990,003082:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019991,003083:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019992,003084: 
019993,003085:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 460 

019995,003087:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019996,003088:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019997,003089:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019998,003090:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019999,003091:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020000,003092:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020001,003093:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020002,003094:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020003,003095:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020004,003096: 
020005,003097:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020006,003098:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020007,003099:

020009,003101: 
020010,003102:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020120,003212:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020121,003213:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020122,003214:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020123,003215:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020124,003216:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020125,003217: 
020126,003218: 
020127,003219:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020128,003220:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020129,003221:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020130,003222:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020131,003223:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020132,003224: 
020133,003225: 
020134,003226:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020135,003227:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020136,003228:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020137,003229:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020138,003230:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020139,003231:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020140,003232:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020141,003233:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020142,003234:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020143,003235:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020144,003236: 
020145,003237: 
020146,003238:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 463 

020148,003240:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020149,003241:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020150,003242:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020151,003243:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020152,003244:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020153,003245: 
020154,003246:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020155,003247:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020156,003248:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020157,003249:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020158,003250:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020159,003251:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020160,003252:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020161,003253:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020162,003254:

020209,003301: 
020210,003302: 
020211,003303:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
020212,003304:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
020213,003305:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.

020215,003307:

020217,003309:
