020506,003598:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
020507,003599: 
020508,003600:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
020509,003601:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
020510,003602:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
020511,003603:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
020512,003604: 
020513,003605:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020514,003606:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
020515,003607:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
020516,003608:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
020517,003609:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020518,003610:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
020519,003611:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
020520,003612: 
020521,003613: 
020522,003614:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
020523,003615:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
020524,003616:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
020525,003617:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
020526,003618:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
020527,003619: 
020528,003620: 
020529,003621:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
020530,003622:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020531,003623:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020532,003624:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020533,003625:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020534,003626: 
020535,003627: 
020536,003628:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020537,003629:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
020538,003630:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
020539,003631: 
020540,003632: 
020541,003633:                                                                                                  #  .
020542,003634: 
020543,003635: 
020544,003636:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020545,003637:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020546,003638:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL
020547,003639:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020548,003640: 
020549,003641: 
020550,003642:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020551,003643:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020552,003644:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020553,003645:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020554,003646:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
020555,003647:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 472 

020557,003649:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020558,003650: 
020559,003651:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020560,003652:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
020561,003653:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020562,003654:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
020563,003655:    4443           10641                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
020564,003656:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
020565,003657: 
020566,003658:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
020567,003659:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
020568,003660: 
020569,003661: 04,2641                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
020570,003662: 04,2641                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020571,003663: 04,2641           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
020572,003664: 04,2642           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.

020579,003671: 
020580,003672:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
020581,003673:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
020582,003674:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
020583,003675:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
020584,003676:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.

020596,003688:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

020598,003690:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.

020757,003849:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020758,003850:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020759,003851:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020760,003852:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020761,003853:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
020762,003854:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020763,003855:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
020764,003856: 
020765,003857: 40,3655                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2                         
020766,003858: 40,3655                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020768,003860: 40,3656           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.
020769,003861: 40,3657           00004                           INHINT

020774,003866: 40,3664           71035                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
